 The Cobrappost website has exposed the alleged scam of Rs 31,000 crore
 cobrapost kaa kahana he ki saarvajanik rup se uplabdh dastavezon ke vishleshan se hi ghotaale kaa pataa chalata he
 This money is not the money of any company, but the money of the public, which is formed and put into the account of different companies, these companies also belong to the same promoter who gives the loan money to them
 cobra kaa maananaa he ki yah bhartiya itihaas kaa sabase bada banking ghotaalaa he
 The character of Cobrapost plays an organization called DHFL
 jisane kai shell companiyon ko lone diya, grant diya
 The money was then taken out of India through these companies
 unase sampatti khridi gai
 The Cobrapost report captures the role of the promoter of Dewan Housing Finance Corporation Limited (DHFL)
 iske hissedaar (stakeholders) kapil vadhvan, aruna vadhvan or dhiraj vadhvan kii kai shell companiyaan hai jise DHFL se lone diya jaataa he
 With this money, shares and properties are purchased in Mauritius, Sri Lanka, Dubai, UK
 isse pataa chalata he ki bharat kaa vittiya system kitna khokhla ho chukaa he
 Loans worth crores are issued without guarantee
 lone dene se pehle niyamon kaa paalan nahin hota or na hi dene ke baad hota he
 DHFL gives loans to these shell companies without any deep investigation
 in companiyon yaa inke nideshkon ke naam kisi prakaar kii koi sampatti nahin he
 It is difficult to repay the loan
 is paise se vadhvan samooh kathith rup se nijee sampatti banaata he
 Public sector banks will have to bear the loss of this
 state bank aaf india or bank of baroda ne 11000 or 4000 karod ne DHFL main lone dekar nivesh kiya he
 We have already seen the scam of IL&FS, due to which wrong policies have given loans of millions of crores to people or companies whose return is difficult
 ab sarkaar ko DHFL kaa bhi adhigrahan karnaa padegaa
 But IL&FS was acquired without investigation
 DHFL main 200 karod se adhik ke lone dene ke liye ek finans cameti he
 The members of this committee are Kapil Badhwan and Dheeraj Badhwan
 in logon ne sunishchit kiya ki hazaron karod ke lone un shell companiyon ko mili, jin par baadhwan kaa niyantran tha
 Dozens of companies were created with a capital of one lakh and they were divided into several companies
 kai companiyon kaa pataa ek hi he
 Their initial directors are also similar
 inaki auditing bhi ek hi group se karai gai he taaki kathith ghotaale par pardaa daalaa ja sake
 Cobrapost has identified 45 companies that were used through Badhawan
 in sabhi 42 companiyon ko 14,282 karod se adhik lone die gaye hai
 Of these, 34 companies are directly under the purview of Badhwan who is the main promoter of DHFL
 jisane bina guarantee ke 10,493 karod kaa lone diya
 There are 11 companies of Sahana Group, which have been given a loan of 3,789 crores
 yah sab cobrapost ne daawa kiya he
 The Post says that the income of 34 companies is neither known nor their business
 cobrapost ne likhaa he ki reserve bank, sebi, vitt mantralay kii naak ke neeche manilaundring kaa khel chalata rahaa
 Neither the Income Tax Department nor the auditing agencies could catch this scam

 He would spend six hours every day taking his spade to break the plateau from which people had to climb
 
 
 uski is avishwasaneey ichhashakti kaa parinaam yah rahaa ki ab vahaan 200-meter kii ek kachi sadak he, jo itani chaudee he ki chote vaahan aaraam se vahaan se guzar sakate hai
 
 
 Shashi told NDTV, "I just kept digging, because people thought i wouldn't be able to
" 
 
 maine sochaa, agar main khodta rahoonga, to na sirf sadak ban jaaegi, balki meri phisiotherapy bhi ho jaaegi
 
 
 " shashi kaa kahana he, "agar panchayat mujhe koi vohan nahin bhi detii he, to bhavishya main kam se kam logon ke paas aane-jane ke liye sadak to hogi
 
 
 " shashi ke pados main rahane vaali 52-varshiya sudhaa sadak coke liye shashi kii shukraguzaar he
 
 
 She says, "it's a lot easier to get around now
" 
 
 ab hamen us oonche pathaar par chadhana nahin padataa
 
 
 i used to worry about watching him dig for hours, but now i am amazed
 
 
 "tippaniyan While narrating his story, there came a time when Shashi's eyes filled up
 
 
 uski patni ne bhi apane or pati ke bhavishya ke bare main sochakar ronaa shuru kar diya
 
 
 She explains, "I used to beg them not to dig like this
" 
 
 agar inhen phir kuch ho jaataa, to hamaare paas ilaak karwaane ke liye paise bhi nahin the
 
 
 We are immersed in heavy debt
 
 
 ab sabhi log ban rahi sadak ke bare main baat karte hai, lekin hamaare bare main kya
 
 
 ? " khayr, khud ko sanyat karte hue shashi muskuraakar kahata he, "bas, ab is sadak kaa kaam khatm karne main mujhe sirf ek maheenaa lagegaa
 
 
 But the panchayat has not given me my three-wheeler yet
 
 
 " So, Shashi started digging himself, and did not stop again
 
 
 vah har rose chah-chah ghante apni kudali lekar us pathaar ko todane main juta rahata, jis par se chadhakar logon ko janaa padataa tha
 
 
 The result of his incredible will is that there is now a 200-meter unpaved road, so wide that small vehicles can pass through it comfortably
 
 
 shashi ne NDTV se kaha, "main bas khodta chalaa gaya, kyonki logon ne sochaa main nahin kar paaungaa
 
 
 i thought, if i keep digging, not only will the road be built, but my physiotherapy will also be done
 
 
 " Shashi says, "if the panchayat does not give me any food, at least in the future there will be a road for people to come and go
 
 
 " The 52-year-old Sudha living in Shashi's neighborhood is thankful to Shashi
 
 
 vah kahati he, "ab aana-janaa bahut aasaan ho gaya he
 
 
 Now we do not have to climb that high plateau
 
 
 main use ghanton tak khudaai karte dekhakar chintaa karti thi, lekin ab main vismit hum
 
 
 "comments apni kahani sunaate-sunaate ek vakt aisa bhi aayaa, jab shashi kii ankhen bhar ain
 
 
 His wife also started crying thinking about her and her husband's future
 
 
 vah bataati he, "main inke saamne gidgidaati thi ki is tarah khudaai na karen
 
 
 If something happens to them again, we did not even have the money to get the area done
 
 
 ham baari karze main duube hue hai

 ?" Well, while restoring himself, Shashi smiles and says, "enough, now it will take me only one month to finish this road work
"
